\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00392}00392\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Specifies\ the\ loss\ function.\ The\ epsilon-\/insensitive\ loss}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00396}00396\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ fit\_intercept\ :\ bool,\ default=True}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00397}00397\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Whether\ or\ not\ to\ fit\ an\ intercept.\ If\ set\ to\ True,\ the\ feature\ vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00398}00398\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ is\ extended\ to\ include\ an\ intercept\ term:\ \`{}[x\_1,\ ...,\ x\_n,\ 1]\`{},\ where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00399}00399\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1\ corresponds\ to\ the\ intercept.\ If\ set\ to\ False,\ no\ intercept\ will\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00400}00400\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ used\ in\ calculations\ (i.e.\ data\ is\ expected\ to\ be\ already\ centered).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00401}00401\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00402}00402\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ intercept\_scaling\ :\ float,\ default=1.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00403}00403\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ \`{}fit\_intercept\`{}\ is\ True,\ the\ instance\ vector\ x\ becomes\ \`{}[x\_1,\ ...,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00404}00404\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\_n,\ intercept\_scaling]\`{},\ i.e.\ a\ "{}synthetic"{}\ feature\ with\ a\ constant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00405}00405\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ value\ equal\ to\ \`{}intercept\_scaling\`{}\ is\ appended\ to\ the\ instance\ vector.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00406}00406\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ intercept\ becomes\ intercept\_scaling\ *\ synthetic\ feature\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00407}00407\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ liblinear\ internally\ penalizes\ the\ intercept,\ treating\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00408}00408\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ like\ any\ other\ term\ in\ the\ feature\ vector.\ To\ reduce\ the\ impact\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00409}00409\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ regularization\ on\ the\ intercept,\ the\ \`{}intercept\_scaling\`{}\ parameter\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00410}00410\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ be\ set\ to\ a\ value\ greater\ than\ 1;\ the\ higher\ the\ value\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00411}00411\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}intercept\_scaling\`{},\ the\ lower\ the\ impact\ of\ regularization\ on\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00412}00412\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Then,\ the\ weights\ become\ \`{}[w\_x\_1,\ ...,\ w\_x\_n,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00414}00414\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ feature\ weights\ and\ the\ intercept\ weight\ is\ scaled\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00415}00415\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}intercept\_scaling\`{}.\ This\ scaling\ allows\ the\ intercept\ term\ to\ have\ a}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_2__classes_8py_source_l00417}00417\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
